=== SESSION 3 ===
Date: 2026-05-03
Feature completed: API-2 - REST API contract surface for SRS-API-001
Status: 117 remaining features

What I did:
- Added a new Python package `python/atp_api/` that is the declarative source of truth for
  the operator REST API:
  * `routes.py` defines `Method`, `Capability` (11 buckets), and a `Route` dataclass with
    SRS-traced fields. The 14-route `ROUTES` tuple covers every API-2 capability
    (lifecycle, live designation, kill switch, Hot-Swap, backtest launch/query,
    Reservoir ranking, watchlist config, system status, logs, alerts).
  * `openapi.py` builds a deterministic OpenAPI 3.1 dict from `ROUTES` (pure stdlib).
  * `openapi.json` is the frozen byte-equal snapshot regenerated from `ROUTES`.
  * `BIND_HOST=127.0.0.1` and `AUTH_MODEL=local-single-user` encode the SRS-SEC-002
    loopback policy ("Local single-user deployment controls").
  * `README.md` summarises auth model, capability table, confirmation routes, sample
    curl, and the snapshot regeneration recipe.
- Added `tools/rest_api_check.py` — mirror of `strategy_api_check.py`. Prints "API-2 PASS"
  with 13 evidence bullets (one per capability + snapshot freshness + loopback policy).
  Supports `--update` to rewrite the OpenAPI snapshot from current `ROUTES`.
- Added `tests/test_rest_api.py`: subprocess contract test, route shape walk, capability
  coverage (== set(Capability)), OpenAPI snapshot byte-equality, snapshot determinism,
  loopback policy, kill-switch + live-designation confirmation guards, public docstrings.
- Extended `architecture/runtime_services.json` with a `rest_api` block listing the 11
  required capabilities, the snapshot path, and the loopback/auth policy. Extended
  `tools/architecture_check.py` with `assert_rest_api(config)` so the surface is
  enforced architecturally — `SRS-ARCH-001 PASS` now adds an `atp_api covers 11
  capabilities and binds 127.0.0.1` evidence line.
- Extended `init.sh` to run `python3 tools/rest_api_check.py` after the static-server
  smoke test; `✓ Environment ready` now requires both checks to pass. Cargo-tolerance
  preserved.
- Routes that perform irreversible actions (POST /api/v1/kill-switch, POST
  /api/v1/strategies/{id}/promote-live) carry `requires_confirmation=True` and a
  `confirm` query parameter, traced to SRS-SAFE-001 and SYS-2d respectively.

What I tested (end-to-end, all six verifications):
1. `./init.sh` -> "✓ Environment ready" with both smoke test and "Running REST API
   contract check..." steps shown.
2. `python3 tools/architecture_check.py` -> "SRS-ARCH-001 PASS" with the new rest_api
   evidence line.
3. `python3 tools/rest_api_check.py` -> "API-2 PASS" with 13 evidence bullets (11
   capabilities + snapshot in-sync + loopback policy).
4. `python3 -m unittest tests.test_architecture tests.test_strategy_api
   tests.test_rest_api` -> 21 tests OK.
5. Snapshot determinism: regenerate `render_snapshot()` -> byte-equal (30,006 bytes)
   to `python/atp_api/openapi.json`.
6. Deterministic re-run of the contract script -> identical PASS output.

Known issues / notes for next agent:
- `init.sh` is now stricter. A broken `atp_api` import fails init (intended; matches
  the API-1 precedent of architecture_check failing fast). If a future change to
  `ROUTES` is unintended, `tools/rest_api_check.py --update` regenerates the snapshot.
- Hot-Swap automatic-trigger configuration (drawdown threshold, top-rank/momentum
  enable, 7-day cool-down policy edits) is server-internal in this contract; only
  manual promotion (`POST /api/v1/hot-swap`) and `GET /api/v1/hot-swap/status` are
  REST-exposed. A future feature can add `PUT /api/v1/hot-swap/policy` if needed.
- Confirmation is modeled as a `confirm` query parameter on the route declaration; the
  two-step UX (modal + token) lands with UI-4 / dashboard work.
- API-2 declares the contract only — no real HTTP runtime exists yet. `init.sh` still
  serves the placeholder `python3 -m http.server`. Live handlers come with EXE-1,
  ORCH-1, RESV-1, BT-1, DATA-1, LOG-1, NOTIF-1.
- WebSocket overlap deliberately avoided: API-3 owns `/ws/*`. Re-confirm before adding
  any streaming routes here.
- `architecture/container_manifests.json` is still missing (pre-existing); recommend a
  small architecture-cleanup feature to either remove the reference from
  `architecture_check.py` or commit the file.
- Lowest remaining P1 by ID is API-3 (WebSocket API surface) — same contract-evidence
  pattern should apply: declarative event schema + introspection check + snapshot.
